SELECT p0."Id", p0."CategoryId", p0."CreatedAt", p0."Description", p0."Name", p0."Status", p0."VendorId", v."Id", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id", c."Name", c."ParentId", c."isActive", c.slug, s."Id", s."AvailableValues", s."IsActive", s."IsDefault", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."ReservedStockQty", s."StockQty", s."Id0", s."ImageOrder", s."ImageUrl", s."VariantId"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."Name", p."Status", p."VendorId", COALESCE((
        SELECT avg(r."Rating"::double precision)
        FROM reviews AS r
        WHERE p."Id" = r."ProductId"), 0.0) AS c
    FROM products AS p
    WHERE p."Status" = 'Active'
    ORDER BY COALESCE((
        SELECT avg(r."Rating"::double precision)
        FROM reviews AS r
        WHERE p."Id" = r."ProductId"), 0.0) DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS p0
INNER JOIN vendors AS v ON p0."VendorId" = v."Id"
INNER JOIN categories AS c ON p0."CategoryId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1."Id", p1."AvailableValues", p1."IsActive", p1."IsDefault", p1."Price", p1."ProductId", p1."ReservedStockQty", p1."StockQty", p2."Id" AS "Id0", p2."ImageOrder", p2."ImageUrl", p2."VariantId"
    FROM product_variants AS p1
    LEFT JOIN product_images AS p2 ON p1."Id" = p2."VariantId"
) AS s ON p0."Id" = s."ProductId"
ORDER BY p0.c DESC, p0."Id", v."Id", c."Id", s."Id"
